[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmp6k56xznf[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m reproduce [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the curl library when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing [0m[4;94mfile://[0m[39m URLs. The issue occurs in the `mprintf.c` file's `addbyter` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction, triggered through the `file_do` function when handling a file protocol [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequest. AddressSanitizer reports a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation that overflows an [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m-byte stack-allocated `header` buffer at offset [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m in the `file_do` function [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mframe.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **stack-buffer-overflow** vulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow. The issue involves writing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the bounds of a stack-allocated buffer, which could potentially lead to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory corruption, crashes, or exploitation.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered when processing a specific input that includes a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [4;94mfile://[0m[39m URL pointing to `[0m[35m/proc/self/[0m[95mstatus[0m[39m`. The crash occurs during the following [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequence:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer provides an input containing `[0m[4;94mfile:///proc/self/status`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The `file_do` function in `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mfile.c[0m[39m` processes this file protocol [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequest[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. During processing, `curl_msnprintf` is called to format data into a buffer[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The formatting operation through `formatf` and ultimately `addbyter` attempts to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte at address `[0m[1;36m0x7fe517082be0[0m[39m`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. This address is at offset [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m in the stack frame, which is exactly at the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary of the [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte `header` buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mallocated from offset [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m480[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Frame Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `file_do` function's stack frame contains five objects:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `statbuf` at offsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m176[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m144[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m428[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `xfer_buf` at offsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m240[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m248[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m436[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `xfer_blen` at offsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m272[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m437[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `buffer` at offsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m304[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m360[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m464[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `header` at offsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m480[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m466[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m **← Overflowed buffer**[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe memory access at offset [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m is exactly one byte beyond the end of the `header` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer, indicating an off-by-one error or insufficient buffer size calculation.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is reached through the following call chain:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer entry point[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `fuzz_handle_transfer`[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `curl_multi_perform`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. `curl_msnprintf` → `curl_mvsnprintf` → `formatf` → `addbyter` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere the [0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A [0m[4;94mfile://[0m[39m URL: `[0m[4;94mfile:///proc/self/status`[0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Code Snippets[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause Identified**: Line [0m[1;36m495[0m[39m in `lib/file.c` contains a critical typo [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is used instead of `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` as the buffer size [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameter to `msnprintf`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Buffer Size Mismatch**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `header` buffer is allocated with [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m466[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `no_body` constant string is approximately [0m[1;36m144[0m[39m bytes[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m144[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is passed to `msnprintf`, it allows writing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte buffer boundary[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Overflow Mechanism**:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `addbyter` function in `mprintf.c` checks `infop->length < infop->max` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore writing[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With an incorrect max value of [0m[1;36m144[0m[39m bytes, it permits writes past the actual [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This results in a stack-buffer-overflow at offset [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe exact boundary of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe header buffer at offsets [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m480[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Pattern Consistency**: Throughout the codebase, all other uses of `msnprintf` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly use `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdestination_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, not `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39msource_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Line [0m[1;36m495[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis anomalous.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Critical Logic to Preserve**: [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The file protocol handling logic must remain intact[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Header generation for Content-Length, Last-Modified, and no_body messages must[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to work[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The buffer reuse pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing the same `header` buffer for multiple headers[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be maintained[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Symptoms and Root Causes in the Code[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Symptom**: Stack-buffer-overflow at offset [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m when processing [0m[4;94mfile://[0m[39m URLs with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`no_body` requests[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause**: Line [0m[1;36m495[0m[39m uses `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtelling `msnprintf` it has [0m[1;36m144[0m[39m bytes available when only [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes are allocated[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Secondary Issue**: Even with the correct fix, the formatted message [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m143[0m[39m-char [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno_body string + size formatting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m exceeds [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes, leading to truncation[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Previous Patches[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo previous patches were applied. This is the initial fix attempt.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mImmediate Resolution[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Target**: `lib/file.c`, line [0m[1;36m495[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Change the second parameter of `msnprintf` from `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mno_body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current Code** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m495[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed Code**:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mmsnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[32m"%s [0m[32m([0m[32m%ld bytes[0m[32m)[0m[32m \r\n"[0m[39m, no_body, expected_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis single-line change directly addresses the vulnerability by ensuring [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`msnprintf` respects the actual buffer size.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo prevent message truncation and provide a more robust solution, combine the [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Target**: `lib/file.c`, line [0m[1;36m466[0m[39m and line [0m[1;36m495[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m** - Fix the msnprintf parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m495[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mmsnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[32m"%s [0m[32m([0m[32m%ld bytes[0m[32m)[0m[32m \r\n"[0m[39m, no_body, expected_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is optimal**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the evaluation report**:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
